      (adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).requestNonPersonalizedAds=0;

      /** legat.url */
      const legaturl = 'https://allesoffen.de/legat.php';
      /** legat.obstcollector */
      function aobstcollector () {
        let il = document.querySelectorAll('ins');
        // console.log('legat', il);
        if (il.length > 0) {
          var ilc = 0;
          il.forEach(function(ins) {
            (function (o) {
              let mo = new MutationObserver(function(m) {
                m.forEach(function(m) {
                  if (m.attributeName == 'data-ad-status') {
                    if (o.getAttribute('data-ad-status') === 'unfilled') {
                      let lr = (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
                      let ip = o.parentNode;
                      let tk = ip.getAttribute('data-ao-tk_id');
                      let height = ip.getAttribute('data-ao-height');
                      let maxwidth = ip.getAttribute('data-ao-maxwidth');
                      let minwidth = ip.getAttribute('data-ao-minwidth');
                      ilc++;
                      var f = [];
                      f[ilc] = document.createElement('iframe');
                      f[ilc].id = 'legat-' + lr;
                      f[ilc].title = 'Informationsmaterial';
                      f[ilc].src = legaturl + '?ax='+ ilc +'&d=' + lr + ( tk !== undefined && tk !== null && tk !== 'null' ? '&tk_id=' + tk : '' ) +
                        ((height !== undefined && height !== null) ? '&h=' + height : '') + 
                        ((maxwidth !== undefined && maxwidth !== null) ? '&maw=' + maxwidth : '') +
                        ((minwidth !== undefined && minwidth !== null) ? '&miw=' + minwidth : '');
                      f[ilc].style.width = '100%';
                      f[ilc].style.height = (height !== undefined && height !== null) ? height + 'px' : 'auto';
                      f[ilc].style.border = 'none';
                      f[ilc].style.overflow = 'hidden';
                      f[ilc].setAttribute('loading', 'lazy');
                      f[ilc].setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
                      // console.log('container height: ', height, 'file: ', f[ilc].src);
                      o.parentNode.style.backgroundColor='#fff';
                      o.parentNode.style.borderColor='#e7e7e7';
                      o.parentNode.appendChild(f[ilc]);
                      o.remove();
                    }
                  }
                });
              });
              let config = { attributes: true, childList: false, characterData: false };
              mo.observe(o, config);
            })(ins);
          });
        }
      }
    </script>

/** cookie set function */
function cset(val) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime()+(360*24*60*60*1000)); // 360 days
    var expires = "expires="+d.toGMTString();
    document.cookie = val+'=true; expires='+expires+'; path=/; Secure';
}

$(function () {
    /** loading button */
    $('button.btn-loading').on('click', function () {
        let b = $(this);
        let bt_h = b.html();

        let bt_hn = 'Bitte warten ..';
        b.attr('disabled', true);
        b.html(bt_hn);
return false;
    });
});</script>
